     <p><i><b>Star Wars: The Force Awakens</b></i> (also known as <i><b>Star Wars: Episode VII – The Force Awakens</b></i>) is a 2015 American <a href="/wiki/Epic_film" title="Epic film">epic</a> <a href="/wiki/Space_opera" title="Space opera">space opera</a> film directed, co-produced, and co-written by <a href="/wiki/J._J._Abrams" title="J. J. Abrams">J. J. Abrams</a>. The seventh installment in the main <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars" title="Star Wars">Star Wars</a></i> film series, it stars <a href="/wiki/Harrison_Ford" title="Harrison Ford">Harrison Ford</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mark_Hamill" title="Mark Hamill">Mark Hamill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carrie_Fisher" title="Carrie Fisher">Carrie Fisher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Adam_Driver" title="Adam Driver">Adam Driver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Daisy_Ridley" title="Daisy Ridley">Daisy Ridley</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Boyega" title="John Boyega">John Boyega</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Isaac" title="Oscar Isaac">Oscar Isaac</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lupita_Nyong%27o" title="Lupita Nyong'o">Lupita Nyong'o</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andy_Serkis" title="Andy Serkis">Andy Serkis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Domhnall_Gleeson" title="Domhnall Gleeson">Domhnall Gleeson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Daniels" title="Anthony Daniels">Anthony Daniels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Mayhew" title="Peter Mayhew">Peter Mayhew</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Max_von_Sydow" title="Max von Sydow">Max von Sydow</a>. Produced by <a href="/wiki/Lucasfilm" title="Lucasfilm">Lucasfilm</a> and Abrams' <a href="/wiki/Bad_Robot_Productions" title="Bad Robot Productions">Bad Robot Productions</a> and distributed worldwide by <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Studios_Motion_Pictures" title="Walt Disney Studios Motion Pictures">Walt Disney Studios Motion Pictures</a>, <i>The Force Awakens</i> is set 30 years after <i><a href="/wiki/Return_of_the_Jedi" title="Return of the Jedi">Return of the Jedi</a></i>; it follows <a href="/wiki/Rey_(Star_Wars)" title="Rey (Star Wars)">Rey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Finn_(Star_Wars)" title="Finn (Star Wars)">Finn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Poe_Dameron" title="Poe Dameron">Poe Dameron</a>'s search for <a href="/wiki/Luke_Skywalker" title="Luke Skywalker">Luke Skywalker</a> and their fight alongside the Resistance, led by veterans of the <a href="/wiki/Rebel_Alliance" title="Rebel Alliance">Rebel Alliance</a>, against <a href="/wiki/Kylo_Ren" title="Kylo Ren">Kylo Ren</a> and the <a href="/wiki/First_Order_(Star_Wars)" title="First Order (Star Wars)">First Order</a>, a successor group to the <a href="/wiki/Galactic_Empire_(Star_Wars)" title="Galactic Empire (Star Wars)">Galactic Empire</a>.</p> 
     <p><i>The Force Awakens</i> is the first film in the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_sequel_trilogy" title="Star Wars sequel trilogy"><i>Star Wars</i> sequel trilogy</a> announced after Disney's acquisition of Lucasfilm in October 2012. It was produced by Abrams, his longtime collaborator <a href="/wiki/Bryan_Burk" title="Bryan Burk">Bryan Burk</a>, and Lucasfilm president <a href="/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy_(producer)" title="Kathleen Kennedy (producer)">Kathleen Kennedy</a>. Abrams and <a href="/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan" title="Lawrence Kasdan">Lawrence Kasdan</a>, co-writer of the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars#Original_trilogy" title="Star Wars">original trilogy</a> films <i><a href="/wiki/The_Empire_Strikes_Back" title="The Empire Strikes Back">The Empire Strikes Back</a></i> (1980) and <i>Return of the Jedi</i> (1983), rewrote an initial script by <a href="/wiki/Michael_Arndt" title="Michael Arndt">Michael Arndt</a>. <a href="/wiki/John_Williams" title="John Williams">John Williams</a>, composer for the previous six films, returned to compose its <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_(soundtrack)" title="Star Wars: The Force Awakens (soundtrack)">score</a>. <i>Star Wars</i> creator <a href="/wiki/George_Lucas" title="George Lucas">George Lucas</a> served as <a href="/wiki/Creative_consultant" title="Creative consultant">creative consultant</a> during the film's early production. Filming began in April 2014 in <a href="/wiki/Emirate_of_Abu_Dhabi" title="Emirate of Abu Dhabi">Abu Dhabi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">Iceland</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Principal_photography" title="Principal photography">principal photography</a> also taking place in <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Ireland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pinewood_Studios" title="Pinewood Studios">Pinewood Studios</a> in <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, and concluded in November 2014. It is the first <a href="/wiki/Live_action" title="Live action">live-action film</a> in the franchise since <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_%E2%80%93_Revenge_of_the_Sith" title="Star Wars: Episode III – Revenge of the Sith">Star Wars: Episode III – Revenge of the Sith</a></i>, released in 2005.</p> 
     <p><i>Star Wars: The Force Awakens</i> was widely anticipated, with Disney backing the film through extensive marketing campaigns.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> It premiered in Los Angeles on December 14, 2015, four days before its release in North America. Many critics praised the film and compared it favorably to the original trilogy. The film has since broken <a href="/wiki/List_of_box_office_records_set_by_Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens" title="List of box office records set by Star Wars: The Force Awakens">many box office records</a>, becoming the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars#Reception" title="Star Wars">highest-grossing installment of the franchise</a>, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_highest-grossing_films_in_Canada_and_the_United_States" title="List of highest-grossing films in Canada and the United States">highest grossing film in North America</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/List_of_highest-grossing_films" title="List of highest-grossing films">third highest grossing film of all time</a> with a worldwide gross of more than $2 billion.<sup id="cite_ref-.27The_Force_Awakens.27_Is_Now_The_Top-Grossing_.27Star_Wars.27_Film_Ever_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-.27The_Force_Awakens.27_Is_Now_The_Top-Grossing_.27Star_Wars.27_Film_Ever-5">[5]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> It received five <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Academy Award</a> nominations and four <a href="/wiki/British_Academy_Film_Awards" title="British Academy Film Awards">British Academy Film Award</a> nominations, where it won <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Award_for_Best_Special_Visual_Effects" title="BAFTA Award for Best Special Visual Effects">Best Special Visual Effects</a>. Two sequels, <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII" title="Star Wars: Episode VIII">Episode VIII</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_sequel_trilogy#Episode_IX" title="Star Wars sequel trilogy">Episode IX</a></i>, are scheduled for 2017 and 2019 respectively.</p> 
     <p></p>

     <p></p> 
     <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Plot">Plot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Plot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
     <p>Approximately 30 years after the destruction of the second <a href="/wiki/Death_Star" title="Death Star">Death Star</a>, the last remaining <a href="/wiki/Jedi" title="Jedi">Jedi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luke_Skywalker" title="Luke Skywalker">Luke Skywalker</a>, has disappeared. The <a href="/wiki/First_Order_(Star_Wars)" title="First Order (Star Wars)">First Order</a> has risen from the fallen <a href="/wiki/Galactic_Empire_(Star_Wars)" title="Galactic Empire (Star Wars)">Galactic Empire</a> and seeks to eliminate the <a href="/wiki/New_Republic_(Star_Wars)" title="New Republic (Star Wars)">New Republic</a>. The Resistance, backed by the Republic and led by Luke's twin sister, <a href="/wiki/Princess_Leia" title="Princess Leia">General Leia Organa</a>, opposes them while searching for Luke to enlist his aid.</p> 
     <p>Resistance pilot <a href="/wiki/Poe_Dameron" title="Poe Dameron">Poe Dameron</a> meets village elder Lor San Tekka on the planet <a href="/wiki/List_of_Star_Wars_planets_and_moons" title="List of Star Wars planets and moons">Jakku</a> to obtain a map to Luke's location. <a href="/wiki/Stormtrooper_(Star_Wars)" title="Stormtrooper (Star Wars)">Stormtroopers</a> commanded by <a href="/wiki/Kylo_Ren" title="Kylo Ren">Kylo Ren</a> destroy the village and capture Poe. Poe's droid <a href="/wiki/BB-8" title="BB-8">BB-8</a> escapes with the map, and encounters the scavenger <a href="/wiki/Rey_(Star_Wars)" title="Rey (Star Wars)">Rey</a> near a junkyard settlement. Ren tortures Poe using the Force, and learns of BB-8. Stormtrooper <a href="/wiki/Finn_(Star_Wars)" title="Finn (Star Wars)">FN-2187</a>, unable to bring himself to kill for the First Order, frees Poe, and they escape in a stolen <a href="/wiki/TIE_fighter" title="TIE fighter">TIE fighter</a>; Poe dubs FN-2187 "Finn". They crash on Jakku, and Finn survives but is unable to determine if Poe did as well. He encounters Rey and BB-8, but the First Order tracks them and launches an airstrike. Finn, Rey, and BB-8 flee the planet in the <i><a href="/wiki/Millennium_Falcon" title="Millennium Falcon">Millennium Falcon</a></i>, which they steal from a junkyard.</p> 
     <p>The <i>Falcon</i> breaks down and is captured by a larger ship piloted by <a href="/wiki/Han_Solo" title="Han Solo">Han Solo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chewbacca" title="Chewbacca">Chewbacca</a>, looking to reclaim their former vessel. Two rival gangs, seeking to settle debts with Han, board and attack, but Han and company manage to escape in the <i>Falcon</i>. The gangs inform the First Order of the events. At the First Order's Starkiller Base – a planet converted into a superweapon that harnesses energy from stars – Supreme Leader Snoke orders General Hux to use the weapon for the first time. Snoke questions Ren's ability to deal with emotions relating to his father, Han Solo; Ren replies that he means nothing to him.</p> 
     <p>The <i>Falcon</i> crew views BB-8's map and determines it is incomplete. Han explains that Luke attempted to rebuild the Jedi Order but exiled himself when an apprentice turned to the dark side. The crew travels to the planet <a href="/wiki/List_of_Star_Wars_planets_and_moons" title="List of Star Wars planets and moons">Takodana</a> and meet with cantina owner <a href="/wiki/Maz_Kanata" title="Maz Kanata">Maz Kanata</a>, who offers assistance in getting BB-8 to the Resistance. Rey is drawn to a vault on the lower level and finds the <a href="/wiki/Lightsaber" title="Lightsaber">lightsaber</a> that once belonged to Luke and his father <a href="/wiki/Darth_Vader" title="Darth Vader">Anakin Skywalker</a>. She experiences disturbing visions and flees into the woods. Maz gives Finn the lightsaber for safekeeping.</p> 
     <p>Starkiller Base fires and destroys the Republic capital and fleet. The First Order attacks Takodana in search of BB-8. Han, Chewbacca, and Finn are saved by Resistance <a href="/wiki/X-wing_fighter" title="X-wing fighter">X-wing fighters</a> led by Poe, revealing that he survived the earlier crash. Leia arrives at Takodana with <a href="/wiki/C-3PO" title="C-3PO">C-3PO</a> and reunites with Han and Chewbacca. Meahwhile, Ren captures Rey and takes her to Starkiller Base, but when he interrogates her about the map, she is able to resist his mind-reading attempts. Discovering she can use the Force, she escapes using a <a href="/wiki/The_Force_(Star_Wars)" title="The Force (Star Wars)">Jedi mind trick</a> on a nearby guard.</p> 
     <p>At the Resistance base on <a href="/wiki/List_of_Star_Wars_planets_and_moons" title="List of Star Wars planets and moons">D'Qar</a>, BB-8 finds <a href="/wiki/R2-D2" title="R2-D2">R2-D2</a>, who has been inactive since Luke's disappearance. As Starkiller Base prepares to fire on D'Qar, the Resistance devises a plan to destroy the superweapon by attacking a critical facility. Leia urges Han to return their son alive. Using the <i>Falcon</i>, Han, Chewbacca, and Finn infiltrate the facility and plant explosives. Han confronts Ren, calling him by his birth name, Ben, and implores him to abandon the dark side. Ren kills Han, enraging Chewbacca who fires and hits Ren. He sets off the explosives, allowing the Resistance to attack and destroy Starkiller Base.</p> 
     <p>The injured Ren pursues Finn and Rey to the surface. A lightsaber battle between Ren and Finn ensues, leaving Finn badly wounded. Rey takes the lightsaber and uses the Force to defeat Ren, before they are separated by a fissure as the planet begins to disintegrate. Snoke orders Hux to evacuate and bring Ren to him. Rey and Chewbacca escape with Finn in the <i>Falcon</i>. On D'Qar, the Resistance celebrates while Leia, Chewbacca, and Rey mourn Han's death. R2-D2 awakens and reveals the rest of the map, which Rey follows with R2-D2 and Chewbacca to a distant planet. She finds Luke and presents him with the lightsaber.</p> 
     <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cast">Cast</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Cast">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

         <a href="/wiki/File:Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/150px-Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" width="150" height="214" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/225px-Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/300px-Oscar_Isaac_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1808" data-file-height="2574"></a>

        <a href="/wiki/Adam_Driver" title="Adam Driver">Adam Driver</a> as the dark warrior 
        <a href="/wiki/Kylo_Ren" title="Kylo Ren">Kylo Ren</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Daisy_Ridley" title="Daisy Ridley">Daisy Ridley</a> as the scavenger 
        <a href="/wiki/Rey_(Star_Wars)" title="Rey (Star Wars)">Rey</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/John_Boyega" title="John Boyega">John Boyega</a> as the reformed stormtrooper 
        <a href="/wiki/Finn_(Star_Wars)" title="Finn (Star Wars)">Finn</a>, and 
        <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Isaac" title="Oscar Isaac">Oscar Isaac</a> as 
        <a href="/wiki/X-wing_fighter" title="X-wing fighter">X-wing fighter</a> pilot 
        <a href="/wiki/Poe_Dameron" title="Poe Dameron">Poe Dameron</a>.
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Daisy_Ridley" title="Daisy Ridley">Daisy Ridley</a> as <a href="/wiki/Rey_(Star_Wars)" title="Rey (Star Wars)">Rey</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A scavenger abandoned as a child on the desert planet Jakku, who is waiting for her family to return.
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup> Ridley said: "She's completely self-sufficient and does everything for herself, until she meets [Finn] and an adventure begins."
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup> Cailey Fleming plays a young Rey.
       <sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/John_Boyega" title="John Boyega">John Boyega</a> as <a href="/wiki/Finn_(Star_Wars)" title="Finn (Star Wars)">Finn</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A reformed First Order 
       <a href="/wiki/Stormtrooper_(Star_Wars)" title="Stormtrooper (Star Wars)">stormtrooper</a>.
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup>
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastBoyega1_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastBoyega1-9">[9]</a></sup> Boyega said that he learned he obtained the part "over a nice breakfast in 
       <a href="/wiki/Mayfair" title="Mayfair">Mayfair</a>" where Abrams told him: "John, you're the new star of 
       <i>Star Wars</i>."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastBoyega2_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastBoyega2-10">[10]</a></sup> Boyega said: "When we find Finn, he's in incredible danger. And the way he reacts to this danger changes his life, and launches him into the 
       <i>Star Wars</i> universe in a very unique way."
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup> He said in another interview: "He's been taught about [Luke], he knows about his history. For him it's like joining the army and then learning about one of the great enemies of your country."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastHamill1_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastHamill1-11">[11]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Harrison_Ford" title="Harrison Ford">Harrison Ford</a> as <a href="/wiki/Han_Solo" title="Han Solo">Han Solo</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A rogue and a smuggler, formerly a key player in the 
       <a href="/wiki/Rebel_Alliance" title="Rebel Alliance">Rebel Alliance</a>. Ford said Han "does not aspire to the position of 
       <a href="/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi" title="Obi-Wan Kenobi">Obi-Wan</a>, nor do I aspire to be some New Age 
       <a href="/wiki/Alec_Guinness" title="Alec Guinness">Alec Guinness</a>. His development is consistent with the character, and there are emotional elements which have occasioned his growth... There's a lot of the rogue still left in Solo. Some things don't change..."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastFord1_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastFord1-12">[12]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Carrie_Fisher" title="Carrie Fisher">Carrie Fisher</a> as <a href="/wiki/Princess_Leia" title="Princess Leia">General Leia Organa</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       The former princess of the destroyed planet 
       <a href="/wiki/Alderaan" title="Alderaan">Alderaan</a>, turned General of the Resistance, and Luke's twin sister.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastFisher1_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastFisher1-13">[13]</a></sup> After the events of 
       <i>Return of the Jedi</i>, she is described as "a little more battle weary, a little more broken hearted."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastFisher2_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastFisher2-14">[14]</a></sup> Fisher described Leia as "Solitary. Under a lot of pressure. Committed as ever to her cause, but I would imagine feeling somewhat defeated, tired, and pissed." Abrams said: "The stakes are pretty high in the story for her, so there's not much goofing around where Leia's concerned."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastFisher3_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastFisher3-15">[15]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Adam_Driver" title="Adam Driver">Adam Driver</a> as <a href="/wiki/Kylo_Ren" title="Kylo Ren">Kylo Ren</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A dark warrior strong with the Force, originally a member of the Knights of Ren, a son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, and commander of the First Order.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastDriver1_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastDriver1-16">[16]</a></sup>
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastDriver2_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastDriver2-17">[17]</a></sup> Driver said the team tried "not to think of him as being bad, or evil, or a villain. Something that was more three-dimensional. He's more dangerous and unpredictable, and morally justified in doing what he thinks is right."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastDriver3_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastDriver3-18">[18]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Oscar_Isaac" title="Oscar Isaac">Oscar Isaac</a> as <a href="/wiki/Poe_Dameron" title="Poe Dameron">Poe Dameron</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A Resistance 
       <a href="/wiki/X-wing_fighter" title="X-wing fighter">X-wing fighter</a> pilot.
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup>
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastNyongo_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastNyongo-19">[19]</a></sup> Isaac said: "He's the best freaking pilot in the galaxy... He's been sent on a mission by a certain princess, and he ends up coming up across [Finn], and their fates are forever intertwined."
       <sup id="cite_ref-EW10Things_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EW10Things-7">[7]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Lupita_Nyong%27o" title="Lupita Nyong'o">Lupita Nyong'o</a> as <a href="/wiki/Maz_Kanata" title="Maz Kanata">Maz Kanata</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A wise and perceptive figure operating a somewhat shady cantina on the peaceful forest planet, Takodana.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastNyongo_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastNyongo-19">[19]</a></sup> J.J. Abrams said Kanata has "lived over a thousand years. She's had this watering hole … and it's like another bar that you'd find in a corner of the 
       <i>Star Wars</i> universe."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastNyongo2_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastNyongo2-20">[20]</a></sup> According to Abrams, the character was based on his former high school English teacher, Rose Gilbert, who lectured at the 
       <a href="/wiki/Palisades_Charter_High_School" title="Palisades Charter High School">Palisades Charter High School</a> from 1961 to 2013. Abrams said the team "really wanted the story to feel authentic, despite being a wild fantasy. I mentioned Rose in an early story meeting as a sort of timeless, wise figure that I'd actually known in my life."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastNyongo3_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastNyongo3-21">[21]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Mark_Hamill" title="Mark Hamill">Mark Hamill</a> as <a href="/wiki/Luke_Skywalker" title="Luke Skywalker">Luke Skywalker</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       One of the last remaining 
       <a href="/wiki/Jedi" title="Jedi">Jedi</a>, who has gone into hiding. Regarding Luke, Han, and Leia, Abrams stated: "They'd be as old and as mythic as the tale of 
       <a href="/wiki/King_Arthur" title="King Arthur">King Arthur</a>. They would be characters who [the new characters] may have heard of, but maybe not. They'd be characters who they might believe existed, or just sounded like a fairy tale..."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastHamill1_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastHamill1-11">[11]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Andy_Serkis" title="Andy Serkis">Andy Serkis</a> as Supreme Leader Snoke:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       The political leader of the First Order. He is Kylo Ren's master and is very powerful in the 
       <a href="/wiki/Dark_side_(Star_Wars)" title="Dark side (Star Wars)" class="mw-redirect">dark side</a>.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastSerkis1_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastSerkis1-22">[22]</a></sup> Serkis described Snoke as "quite an enigmatic character, and strangely vulnerable at the same time as being quite powerful... He is large. He appears tall. And also just the facial design—you couldn't have gotten there with prosthetics... Without giving too much away at this point, he has a very distinctive, idiosyncratic bone and facial structure."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastSerkis2_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastSerkis2-23">[23]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Domhnall_Gleeson" title="Domhnall Gleeson">Domhnall Gleeson</a> as General Hux:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       The commander of the First Order's Starkiller Base.
       <sup id="cite_ref-GleesonAndPegg_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GleesonAndPegg-24">[24]</a></sup> Gleeson described him as "pretty ruthless. A strong disciplinarian would be a mild way of putting it... He's kind of opposite Kylo Ren. They have their own relationship, which is individual and unusual. One of them is strong in different ways than the other. They're both vying for power."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastGleeson1_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastGleeson1-25">[25]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Anthony_Daniels" title="Anthony Daniels">Anthony Daniels</a> as <a href="/wiki/C-3PO" title="C-3PO">C-3PO</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A humanoid 
       <a href="/wiki/Droid_(robot)" title="Droid (robot)">protocol droid</a> under Organa's service. Daniels said the actors were allowed to experiment with their performances, and that Abrams "made a field, a playpen where you were allowed to take your time and suggest things."
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastDaniels1_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastDaniels1-26">[26]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Mayhew" title="Peter Mayhew">Peter Mayhew</a> as <a href="/wiki/Chewbacca" title="Chewbacca">Chewbacca</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A loyal 
       <a href="/wiki/Wookiee" title="Wookiee">Wookiee</a> and Solo's longtime companion. 
       <a href="/wiki/Joonas_Suotamo" title="Joonas Suotamo">Joonas Suotamo</a> portrays the character in several action scenes, as the 71-year-old Mayhew suffered from knee problems.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastMayhew_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastMayhew-27">[27]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Max_von_Sydow" title="Max von Sydow">Max von Sydow</a> as Lor San Tekka:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       A retired adventurer on Jakku, aiding the Resistance in locating Skywalker.
       <sup id="cite_ref-CastSydow_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CastSydow-28">[28]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <ul> 
      <li><a href="/wiki/Gwendoline_Christie" title="Gwendoline Christie">Gwendoline Christie</a> as <a href="/wiki/Captain_Phasma" title="Captain Phasma">Captain Phasma</a>:</li> 
     </ul> 
     <dl> 
      <dd>
       The commander of the First Order's legions of stormtroopers.
       <sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup>
      </dd> 
     </dl> 
     <p><a href="/wiki/Timothy_M._Rose" title="Timothy M. Rose">Tim Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mike_Quinn_(puppeteer)" title="Mike Quinn (puppeteer)">Mike Quinn</a> reprise their respective roles as <a href="/wiki/Admiral_Ackbar" title="Admiral Ackbar">Admiral Ackbar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nien_Nunb" title="Nien Nunb">Nien Nunb</a>, both from <i>Return of the Jedi</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> Kipsang Rotich returns as the voice of Nien Nunb<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Erik_Bauersfeld" title="Erik Bauersfeld">Erik Bauersfeld</a> returns to voice Ackbar.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kenny_Baker_(English_actor)" title="Kenny Baker (English actor)">Kenny Baker</a>, originally announced as part of the cast, was credited as "consultant" for <a href="/wiki/R2-D2" title="R2-D2">R2-D2</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OfficialCast_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OfficialCast-34">[34]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ewan_McGregor" title="Ewan McGregor">Ewan McGregor</a> has an uncredited vocal <a href="/wiki/Cameo_appearance" title="Cameo appearance">cameo</a> as <a href="/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi" title="Obi-Wan Kenobi">Obi-Wan Kenobi</a> in Rey's vision sequence, while archival audio of <a href="/wiki/Frank_Oz" title="Frank Oz">Frank Oz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alec_Guinness" title="Alec Guinness">Alec Guinness</a> as <a href="/wiki/Yoda" title="Yoda">Yoda</a> and Kenobi, respectively, are also used in the same scene; Oz recorded new dialogue for the film, but it was replaced with pre-existing audio from <i>The Empire Strikes Back</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup></p> 
     <p><a href="/wiki/Dave_Chapman_(actor)" title="Dave Chapman (actor)">Dave Chapman</a> and Brian Herring served as puppeteers for <a href="/wiki/BB-8" title="BB-8">BB-8</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> with <a href="/wiki/Bill_Hader" title="Bill Hader">Bill Hader</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ben_Schwartz" title="Ben Schwartz">Ben Schwartz</a> credited as "Vocal Consultants".<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ken_Leung" title="Ken Leung">Ken Leung</a> appears as Statura, an admiral in the Resistance.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Simon_Pegg" title="Simon Pegg">Simon Pegg</a> appears as Unkar Plutt, the Junkyard dealer on Jakku.<sup id="cite_ref-GleesonAndPegg_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GleesonAndPegg-24">[24]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Greg_Grunberg" title="Greg Grunberg">Greg Grunberg</a> plays Temmin "Snap" Wexley, an X-wing pilot.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kiran_Shah" title="Kiran Shah">Kiran Shah</a> plays Teedo, a scavenger on Jakku who rides a semi-mechanical Luggabeast.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jessica_Henwick" title="Jessica Henwick">Jessica Henwick</a> appears as Jess Testor, an X-wing pilot.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> Brian Vernel appears as Bala-Tik, the leader of the Guavian Death Gang.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-drecord_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-drecord-47">[47]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Yayan_Ruhian" title="Yayan Ruhian">Yayan Ruhian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iko_Uwais" title="Iko Uwais">Iko Uwais</a>, and Cecep Arif Rahman appear as Tasu Leech, Razoo Qin-Fee, and Crokind Shand, members of the Kanjiklub Gang, a criminal organization.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Warwick_Davis" title="Warwick Davis">Warwick Davis</a> appears as Wollivan, a tavern-dweller in Maz Kanata's castle.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Anna_Brewster" title="Anna Brewster">Anna Brewster</a> appears as Bazine Netal, a First Order spy, also at Maz Kanata's castle.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Brodie-Sangster" title="Thomas Brodie-Sangster">Thomas Brodie-Sangster</a><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Kate_Fleetwood" title="Kate Fleetwood">Kate Fleetwood</a><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> play First Order Petty Officers, Thanisson and Unamo, respectively. <a href="/wiki/Billie_Lourd" title="Billie Lourd">Billie Lourd</a>, daughter of Carrie Fisher, appears as Connix, a lieutenant in the Resistance.<sup id="cite_ref-Lourd_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lourd-56">[56]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> Members of the Resistance include <a href="/wiki/Emun_Elliott" title="Emun Elliott">Emun Elliott</a> as Brance<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Maisie_Richardson-Sellers" title="Maisie Richardson-Sellers">Maisie Richardson-Sellers</a> as Korr Sella<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup> while <a href="/wiki/Harriet_Walter" title="Harriet Walter">Harriet Walter</a> appears as Kalonia, the doctor who tends to Chewbacca.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DailyBeastCast_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DailyBeastCast-61">[61]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Mark_Stanley" title="Mark Stanley">Mark Stanley</a> appears as a Knight of Ren.<sup id="cite_ref-DailyBeastCast_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DailyBeastCast-61">[61]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Armesto" title="Sebastian Armesto">Sebastian Armesto</a> portrays Lieutenant Mikata and <a href="/wiki/Pip_Torrens" title="Pip Torrens">Pip Torrens</a> portrays Colonel Caplan, both serving the First Order.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Actor <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Craig" title="Daniel Craig">Daniel Craig</a>, composer <a href="/wiki/Michael_Giacchino" title="Michael Giacchino">Michael Giacchino</a> and record producer <a href="/wiki/Nigel_Godrich" title="Nigel Godrich">Nigel Godrich</a> <a href="/wiki/Stormtrooper_(Star_Wars)#Performers" title="Stormtrooper (Star Wars)">cameo as stormtroopers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> Abrams' assistant, Morgan Dameron, appears as a Resistance officer,<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> while his father, <a href="/wiki/Gerald_W._Abrams" title="Gerald W. Abrams">Gerald W. Abrams</a>, appears as Captain Cypress.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup> The film's dialect coach, <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Jack" title="Andrew Jack">Andrew Jack</a>, appears as Major Ematt of the Resistance.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> Additionally, Crystal Clarke, Pip Andersen,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Christina_Chong" title="Christina Chong">Christina Chong</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup> Miltos Yerolemou,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> Amybeth Hargreaves,<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Leanne_Best" title="Leanne Best">Leanne Best</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Judah_Friedlander" title="Judah Friedlander">Judah Friedlander</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Smith" title="Kevin Smith">Kevin Smith</a><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> were cast in minor roles. Abrams has a vocal cameo,<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup> singing with <a href="/wiki/Lin-Manuel_Miranda" title="Lin-Manuel Miranda">Lin-Manuel Miranda</a> on two songs, "Jabba Flow" and "Dobra Doompa", performed by Shag Kava, consisting of Abrams, Manuel and musicians.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(2008_TV_series)" title="Star Wars: The Clone Wars (2008 TV series)">Star Wars: The Clone Wars</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels" title="Star Wars Rebels">Star Wars Rebels</a></i> cast members <a href="/wiki/Dee_Bradley_Baker" title="Dee Bradley Baker">Dee Bradley Baker</a>, <a href="/wiki/Matt_Lanter" title="Matt Lanter">Matt Lanter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Kane" title="Tom Kane">Tom Kane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Catherine_Taber" title="Catherine Taber">Catherine Taber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Wood_(sound_editor)" title="Matthew Wood (sound editor)">Matthew Wood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sam_Witwer" title="Sam Witwer" class="mw-redirect">Sam Witwer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Meredith_Salenger" title="Meredith Salenger">Meredith Salenger</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Arnold_Taylor" title="James Arnold Taylor">James Arnold Taylor</a> and show runner <a href="/wiki/Dave_Filoni" title="Dave Filoni">Dave Filoni</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/David_Acord" title="David Acord">David Acord</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Donovan" title="Michael Donovan">Michael Donovan</a>, Devon Libran, Elle Newlands, Terri Douglas, Robert Stambler, Verona Blue, TJ Falls, Michelle Rejwan, <a href="/wiki/Eugene_Byrd" title="Eugene Byrd">Eugene Byrd</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Tatasciore" title="Fred Tatasciore">Fred Tatasciore</a>, David Collins, Amanda Foreman, Christopher Scarabosio, Patrick Correll, Karen Huie, Orly Schuchmacher, Emily Towers, Jonathan Dixon, Kat Sheridan, <a href="/wiki/Salacious_Crumb" title="Salacious Crumb" class="mw-redirect">Salacious Crumb</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Mark_Dodson" title="Mark Dodson">Mark Dodson</a>, and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Star_Wars_characters#S" title="List of Star Wars characters">Gavyn Sykes</a> actor Christian Simpson were the additional voices used in the film.<sup id="cite_ref-DailyBeastCast_61-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DailyBeastCast-61">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup></p> 
     <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Production">Production</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Production">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Development">Development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <div role="note" class="hatnote">
      See also: 
      <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_sequel_trilogy" title="Star Wars sequel trilogy">Star Wars sequel trilogy</a>
     </div> 
     <p><i>Star Wars</i> creator <a href="/wiki/George_Lucas" title="George Lucas">George Lucas</a> discussed ideas for a <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_sequel_trilogy" title="Star Wars sequel trilogy">sequel trilogy</a> several times after the conclusion of the original trilogy, but denied any intent to make it.<sup id="cite_ref-LATimes2008_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LATimes2008-79">[79]</a></sup> In October 2012, he sold his production company <a href="/wiki/Lucasfilm" title="Lucasfilm">Lucasfilm</a>, and with it the <i>Star Wars</i> franchise, to <a href="/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company" title="The Walt Disney Company">The Walt Disney Company</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BloombergMar2013_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BloombergMar2013-80">[80]</a></sup> Speaking alongside Lucasfilm's new president, <a href="/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy_(producer)" title="Kathleen Kennedy (producer)">Kathleen Kennedy</a>, Lucas said: "I always said I wasn't going to do any more and that's true, because I'm not going to do any more, but that doesn't mean I'm unwilling to turn it over to Kathy to do more."<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>As creative consultant on the film, Lucas attended early story meetings and advised on the details of the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_expanded_universe" title="Star Wars expanded universe"><i>Star Wars</i> universe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BloombergMar2013_80-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BloombergMar2013-80">[80]</a></sup> Among the materials he turned over to the production team were his rough <a href="/wiki/Film_treatment" title="Film treatment">story treatments</a> for <i>Episodes VII–IX</i>, which Lucas requested would only be read by Kennedy, <a href="/wiki/Bob_Iger" title="Bob Iger">Bob Iger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alan_F._Horn" title="Alan F. Horn">Alan Horn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kevin_A._Mayer" title="Kevin A. Mayer">Kevin Mayer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup> Lucas later stated that Disney had discarded his story ideas<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Lucas_treatment_unused_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lucas_treatment_unused-84">[84]</a></sup> and that he had no further involvement with the film.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> Lucas' son Jett told <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> that his father was "very torn" about having sold the rights to the franchise, despite having hand-picked Abrams to direct, and that his father was "there to guide" but that "he wants to let it go and become its new generation."<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In November 2015, Lucas said that Disney was "not that keen" to involve him and conceded: "If I get in there, I'm just going to cause trouble because they're not going to do what I want them to do, and I don't have the control to do that any more, and all it would do is just muck everything up."<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> In December 2015, after the film's release, he said: "They wanted to do a retro movie. I don't like that. Every movie, I worked very hard to make them different&nbsp;... I made them completely different—different planets, different spaceships to make it new."<sup id="cite_ref-NYT-20151231_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYT-20151231-88">[88]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup> Abrams felt that, as the first in a new trilogy, the film "needed to take a couple of steps backwards into very familiar terrain" and use plot elements from previous <i>Star Wars</i> films.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup></p> 
     <div class="thumb tleft"> 
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a href="/wiki/File:Kathleen_Kennedy,_J._J._Abrams,_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/220px-Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/330px-Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/440px-Kathleen_Kennedy%2C_J._J._Abrams%2C_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5616" data-file-height="3744"></a> 
       <div class="thumbcaption"> 
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Kathleen_Kennedy,_J._J._Abrams,_Lawrence_Kasdan_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
        </div> (L–R) Producer 
        <a href="/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy_(producer)" title="Kathleen Kennedy (producer)">Kathleen Kennedy</a>, writer and director 
        <a href="/wiki/J._J._Abrams" title="J. J. Abrams">J. J. Abrams</a> and writer 
        <a href="/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan" title="Lawrence Kasdan">Lawrence Kasdan</a> speaking at the 2015 
        <a href="/wiki/San_Diego_Comic-Con_International" title="San Diego Comic-Con International">San Diego Comic-Con International</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p><i>Episode VII</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">'</span>s first screenplay was written by <a href="/wiki/Michael_Arndt" title="Michael Arndt">Michael Arndt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hiatt_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiatt-94">[94]</a></sup> Early drafts had Luke appear midway through the film, but Arndt found that "every time Luke came in and entered the movie, he just took it over. Suddenly you didn't care about your main character anymore."<sup id="cite_ref-EWDec2015_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EWDec2015-95">[95]</a></sup> Luke became the film's <a href="/wiki/MacGuffin" title="MacGuffin">MacGuffin</a> and does not appear in person until the final scene.<sup id="cite_ref-EWDec2015_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EWDec2015-95">[95]</a></sup> Several directors were considered, including <a href="/wiki/David_Fincher" title="David Fincher">David Fincher</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Brad_Bird" title="Brad Bird">Brad Bird</a><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Guillermo_del_Toro" title="Guillermo del Toro">Guillermo del Toro</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup> After a suggestion by <a href="/wiki/Steven_Spielberg" title="Steven Spielberg">Steven Spielberg</a> to Kennedy,<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/J._J._Abrams" title="J. J. Abrams">J. J. Abrams</a> was named director in January 2013, with <a href="/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan" title="Lawrence Kasdan">Lawrence Kasdan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Simon_Kinberg" title="Simon Kinberg">Simon Kinberg</a> as project consultants.<sup id="cite_ref-StarWarsComJan2013_100-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-StarWarsComJan2013-100">[100]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Arndt worked on the script for eight months, but said he needed 18 more, which was more time than Disney or Abrams could give him.<sup id="cite_ref-Hiatt_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiatt-94">[94]</a></sup> The production announced Arndt's exit from the project on October 24, 2013, and Kasdan and Abrams took over script duties.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> Abrams expressed relief that the release date was announced for December 2015 instead of a previously discussed summer release.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup> He and Kasdan planned the story while walking in <a href="/wiki/Santa_Monica,_California" title="Santa Monica, California">Santa Monica</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> and <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. The first draft was completed in six weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup> Abrams said that the key for the film was to return to the roots of the first <i>Star Wars</i> film and be based more on emotion than explanation.<sup id="cite_ref-Parismatch_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Parismatch-105">[105]</a></sup> In January 2014, Abrams confirmed that the script was complete.<sup id="cite_ref-WrapScript_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WrapScript-106">[106]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>A fictional language was developed for use in the film by <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> star <a href="/wiki/Sara_Maria_Forsberg" title="Sara Maria Forsberg" class="mw-redirect">Sara Maria Forsberg</a>, who created the <a href="/wiki/Viral_video" title="Viral video">viral video</a> series "What Languages Sound Like To Foreigners";<sup id="cite_ref-forsberg_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-forsberg-107">[107]</a></sup> Forsberg developed the language by studying languages such as <a href="/wiki/Hindi" title="Hindi">Hindi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gujarati_language" title="Gujarati language">Gujarati</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-forsberg_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-forsberg-107">[107]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In April 2014, Lucasfilm clarified that <i>Episodes VII–IX</i> would not feature storylines from the <a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_expanded_universe" title="Star Wars expanded universe">expanded universe</a>, though other elements could be included as with the TV series <i>Star Wars Rebels</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-EUApril2014_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EUApril2014-108">[108]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Abrams stated that he purposely withheld some plot elements from <i>Episode VII</i>, such as Finn and Rey's last names and their backgrounds. Kennedy admitted that "we haven't mapped out every single detail [of the sequel trilogy] yet", but said that Abrams is collaborating with <i>Episode VIII</i> director <a href="/wiki/Rian_Johnson" title="Rian Johnson">Rian Johnson</a>, and then Johnson will work with <i>Episode IX</i> director <a href="/wiki/Colin_Trevorrow" title="Colin Trevorrow">Colin Trevorrow</a>, to ensure a smooth transition and "that everybody's got a say in how we move forward with this".<sup id="cite_ref-Variety7Dec2015_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Variety7Dec2015-109">[109]</a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pre-production">Pre-production</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Pre-production">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <p>In May 2013, it was confirmed that <i>Episode VII</i> would be filmed in the United Kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-StarWarsComUKMay2013_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-StarWarsComUKMay2013-110">[110]</a></sup> Representatives from Lucasfilm met with <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_the_Exchequer" title="Chancellor of the Exchequer">Chancellor of the Exchequer</a> <a href="/wiki/George_Osborne" title="George Osborne">George Osborne</a> to agree to produce <i>Episode VII</i> in the UK.<sup id="cite_ref-StarWarsComUKMay2013_110-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-StarWarsComUKMay2013-110">[110]</a></sup> Osborne committed £25 million ($37 million) of public money towards the film, claiming it was a boost for British culture and the film industry.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Beginning in September 2013, production spaces at the <a href="/wiki/Bad_Robot_Productions" title="Bad Robot Productions">Bad Robot</a> facility were converted for shooting of <i>Episode VII</i> for the benefit of shooting a minor portion of the film in the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>The film's costume designer was <a href="/wiki/Michael_Kaplan_(costume_designer)" title="Michael Kaplan (costume designer)">Michael Kaplan</a>, who had previously worked with Abrams on <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_(film)" title="Star Trek (film)">Star Trek</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Into_Darkness" title="Star Trek Into Darkness">Star Trek Into Darkness</a></i> films.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> Film editors <a href="/wiki/Mary_Jo_Markey" title="Mary Jo Markey">Mary Jo Markey</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maryann_Brandon" title="Maryann Brandon">Maryann Brandon</a>, also long-term collaborators with Abrams, were also signed.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> In August 2013, it was announced that <a href="/wiki/Cinematographer" title="Cinematographer">cinematographer</a> <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Mindel" title="Daniel Mindel" class="mw-redirect">Daniel Mindel</a> would be shooting the film on <a href="/wiki/35_mm_film" title="35 mm film">35 mm film</a> (specifically <a href="/wiki/Eastman_Kodak" title="Eastman Kodak" class="mw-redirect">Kodak</a> <a href="/wiki/Vision_3" title="Vision 3" class="mw-redirect">5219</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup> In October 2013, other crew members were confirmed, including sound designer <a href="/wiki/Ben_Burtt" title="Ben Burtt">Ben Burtt</a>, director of photography Daniel Mindel, production designers <a href="/wiki/Rick_Carter" title="Rick Carter">Rick Carter</a> and Darren Gilford, costume designer Michael Kaplan, special effects supervisor <a href="/wiki/Chris_Corbould" title="Chris Corbould">Chris Corbould</a>, re-recording mixer <a href="/wiki/Gary_Rydstrom" title="Gary Rydstrom">Gary Rydstrom</a>, supervising sound editor Matthew Wood, visual effects supervisor Roger Guyett, and executive producers Tommy Harper and Jason McGatlin.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Casting">Casting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Casting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <div class="thumb tright"> 
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a href="/wiki/File:Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/220px-Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/330px-Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg/440px-Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5616" data-file-height="3744"></a> 
       <div class="thumbcaption"> 
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Star_Wars_-_The_Force_Awakens_cast_by_Gage_Skidmore.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
        </div> The cast of 
        <i>Star Wars: The Force Awakens</i> at the 2015 San Diego Comic Con International (L–R: 
        <a href="/wiki/John_Boyega" title="John Boyega">John Boyega</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Daisy_Ridley" title="Daisy Ridley">Daisy Ridley</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Isaac" title="Oscar Isaac">Oscar Isaac</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Adam_Driver" title="Adam Driver">Adam Driver</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Domhnall_Gleeson" title="Domhnall Gleeson">Domhnall Gleeson</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Gwendoline_Christie" title="Gwendoline Christie">Gwendoline Christie</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Carrie_Fisher" title="Carrie Fisher">Carrie Fisher</a>, 
        <a href="/wiki/Mark_Hamill" title="Mark Hamill">Mark Hamill</a> and 
        <a href="/wiki/Harrison_Ford" title="Harrison Ford">Harrison Ford</a>)
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p>Casting began around August 2013, with Abrams meeting with potential actors for script readings and screen tests. Open auditions were held in the UK, Ireland, and the United States in November 2013 for the roles of Rachel and Thomas.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> Casting began in earnest in January 2014, because of changes to the script by Kasdan and Abrams.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup> Screen tests with actors continued until at least three weeks before the official announcement on April 29, 2014, with final casting decisions made only a few weeks prior. Actors testing had strict non-disclosure agreements, preventing them, their agents or publicists from commenting on their potential involvement.<sup id="cite_ref-secret_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-secret-124">[124]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Though Lucas intimated that previous cast members <a href="/wiki/Carrie_Fisher" title="Carrie Fisher">Carrie Fisher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harrison_Ford" title="Harrison Ford">Harrison Ford</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mark_Hamill" title="Mark Hamill">Mark Hamill</a> would return for the new film as early as March 2013,<sup id="cite_ref-BloombergMar2013_80-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BloombergMar2013-80">[80]</a></sup> their casting was not confirmed until over a year later.<sup id="cite_ref-OfficialCast_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OfficialCast-34">[34]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Saoirse_Ronan" title="Saoirse Ronan">Saoirse Ronan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Michael_B._Jordan" title="Michael B. Jordan">Michael B. Jordan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Lupita_Nyong%27o" title="Lupita Nyong'o">Lupita Nyong'o</a><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup> auditioned for new characters; industry publications reported <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Plemons" title="Jesse Plemons">Jesse Plemons</a> was considered, possibly for Luke Skywalker's son;<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Adam_Driver" title="Adam Driver">Adam Driver</a> for an unnamed villain;<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> and Maisie Richardson-Sellers for an unknown character.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup> In March 2014, actor <a href="/wiki/Dominic_Monaghan" title="Dominic Monaghan">Dominic Monaghan</a> said that Abrams was looking for three unknown actors to play the leads in <i>Episode VII</i> and that rumors of bigger-name stars were untrue.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup></p> 
     <p><a href="/wiki/Daisy_Ridley" title="Daisy Ridley">Daisy Ridley</a> was chosen for the film by February 2014, and by the end of that month a deal had been worked out with Driver, who was able to work around his <i><a href="/wiki/Girls_(TV_series)" title="Girls (TV series)">Girls</a></i> schedule. By March 2014, talks with <a href="/wiki/Andy_Serkis" title="Andy Serkis">Andy Serkis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Isaac" title="Oscar Isaac">Oscar Isaac</a> began and continued into April 2014. In April, <a href="/wiki/John_Boyega" title="John Boyega">John Boyega</a> began talks after dropping out of <a href="/wiki/Race_(2016_film)" title="Race (2016 film)">a Jesse Owens biopic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-secret_124-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-secret-124">[124]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Denis_Lawson" title="Denis Lawson">Denis Lawson</a>, who played <a href="/wiki/Wedge_Antilles" title="Wedge Antilles">Wedge Antilles</a> in the original trilogy, declined to reprise his role, stating that it would have "bored" him.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>On April 29, 2014, the cast was announced with a photo of the first <a href="/wiki/Read-through" title="Read-through">table read</a> of the script at <a href="/wiki/Pinewood_Studios" title="Pinewood Studios">Pinewood Studios</a> near London,<sup id="cite_ref-OfficialCast_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OfficialCast-34">[34]</a></sup> picturing director Abrams with Ford, Ridley, Fisher, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Mayhew" title="Peter Mayhew">Peter Mayhew</a>, producer <a href="/wiki/Bryan_Burk" title="Bryan Burk">Bryan Burk</a>, Lucasfilm president and producer <a href="/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy_(producer)" title="Kathleen Kennedy (producer)">Kathleen Kennedy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Domhnall_Gleeson" title="Domhnall Gleeson">Domhnall Gleeson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Daniels" title="Anthony Daniels">Anthony Daniels</a>, Hamill, Serkis, Oscar Isaac, Boyega, Driver, and writer Lawrence Kasdan. The announcement was originally planned for May 4 (<a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Day" title="Star Wars Day"><i>Star Wars</i> Day</a>), but was announced early for fear of media leaks. In June 2014, cast additions Lupita Nyong'o and Gwendoline Christie were announced.<sup id="cite_ref-OfficialCast2_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OfficialCast2-133">[133]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>To prepare for his role, Hamill grew out his beard<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup> and was assigned a personal trainer and a nutritionist at the request of the producers, who wanted him to resemble an older Luke.<sup id="cite_ref-DigitalSpy_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DigitalSpy-135">[135]</a></sup> Fisher was assigned a personal trainer and a nutritionist.<sup id="cite_ref-DigitalSpy_135-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DigitalSpy-135">[135]</a></sup> Abrams initially considered using Daniels only in a voice role for C-3PO,<sup id="cite_ref-C3POdemand_136-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-C3POdemand-136">[136]</a></sup> but Daniels opted to reprise the role physically as well; the production team built a new C-3PO suit to accommodate him.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In May, Abrams announced a donation contest for <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> from the <i>Star Wars</i> set in Abu Dhabi; the winner was allowed to visit the set, meet members of the cast and appear in the film.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup> In October 2014, Warwick Davis, who played Wald and Weazle in <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_%E2%80%93_The_Phantom_Menace" title="Star Wars: Episode I – The Phantom Menace">The Phantom Menace</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/Wicket_W._Warrick" title="Wicket W. Warrick" class="mw-redirect">Wicket</a> in <i>Return of the Jedi</i>, announced that he would appear in <i>The Force Awakens</i>, but did not reveal his role.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup> In November 2014, <a href="/wiki/Debbie_Reynolds" title="Debbie Reynolds">Debbie Reynolds</a> confirmed that her granddaughter (Fisher's daughter), <a href="/wiki/Billie_Lourd" title="Billie Lourd">Billie Lourd</a>, is in the film.<sup id="cite_ref-Lourd_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lourd-56">[56]</a></sup> Isaac's uncle, a <i>Star Wars</i> fan, was cast as an extra at the invitation of Abrams upon visiting the set.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In December 2015, <i>The Mail</i> reported that Ford will be paid $25 million plus a 0.5% share of the revenue. Ridley and Boyega each will receive $460,000 plus a share if the movie grosses over $1 billion. Fisher received $1.5 million and Abrams was paid $5.1 million plus a 2% share of the revenue. For the original 1977 film, Ford was paid $10,000 (equivalent to $39,000 in 2015).<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Filming">Filming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Filming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <div class="thumb tmulti tleft"> 
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:204px;max-width:204px"> 
       <div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px"> 
        <div class="thumbimage">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Skellig_Michael_(6214838436).jpg" class="image"><img alt="view over Skellig Michael showing stone beehive structures and Small Skellig island in the distance" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg/200px-Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg" width="200" height="135" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg/300px-Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg/400px-Skellig_Michael_%286214838436%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1166" data-file-height="786"></a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px"> 
        <div class="thumbimage">
         <a href="/wiki/File:RAF_Greenham_Common,_silo.jpg" class="image"><img alt="concrete missile silo covered in grass" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg/200px-RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg" width="200" height="114" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg/300px-RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg/400px-RAF_Greenham_Common%2C_silo.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="584"></a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left;text-align:;background-color:">
        <a href="/wiki/Skellig_Michael" title="Skellig Michael">Skellig Michael</a> in Ireland (top) and former 
        <a href="/wiki/RAF_Greenham_Common" title="RAF Greenham Common">RAF Greenham Common</a> in England served as filming locations.
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p>In February 2014, Abrams said filming would begin in May and last about three months.<sup id="cite_ref-Parismatch_105-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Parismatch-105">[105]</a></sup> The official announcement came in March, when Disney and Lucasfilm announced that <a href="/wiki/Principal_photography" title="Principal photography">principal photography</a> would commence in May and be based at Pinewood Studios in <a href="/wiki/Buckinghamshire" title="Buckinghamshire">Buckinghamshire</a>, England.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup> That month, it was revealed that pre-production filming would be taking place in <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">Iceland</a> prior to the start of official filming in May, consisting of landscape shots which would be used for scenery in the film.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup> In April, <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_Studios_(division)" title="Walt Disney Studios (division)">Walt Disney Studios</a> chairman <a href="/wiki/Alan_F._Horn" title="Alan F. Horn">Alan Horn</a> confirmed that filming had begun,<sup id="cite_ref-Appelo_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Appelo-144">[144]</a></sup> filming in secret in the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">U.A.E.</a> <a href="/wiki/Abu_Dhabi_(emirate)" title="Abu Dhabi (emirate)" class="mw-redirect">emirate of Abu Dhabi</a> by a second-unit.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup> Later that month, it was revealed that in addition to 35mm film, segments of the film were being shot in the <a href="/wiki/70_mm_film" title="70 mm film">65mm</a> IMAX format.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup> In July, Bad Robot reported on Twitter that the film would be at least partially shot on <a href="/wiki/IMAX" title="IMAX">IMAX</a> cameras.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>On May 4, 2014 (<a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_Day" title="Star Wars Day"><i>Star Wars</i> Day</a>), the studio posted a <a href="/wiki/Selfie" title="Selfie">selfie</a> taken by Iger with an unidentified actor in a Chewbacca costume.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> Iger stated the photo was taken when he visited Pinewood Studios two weeks earlier to discuss the shoot, "which was just about to start", with Abrams, Kennedy, and Horn.<sup id="cite_ref-Faber_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Faber-150">[150]</a></sup> Principal photography began in Abu Dhabi on May 16, 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup> Abrams and members of the cast went to Abu Dhabi in early May, where large sets were built at the location, including a shuttle-like spacecraft, a large tower and a big market, and explosives were used to create a "blast crater." Cast members were spotted practicing driving vehicles that would be used during filming.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> Production moved to Pinewood Studios in June.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In June, Harrison Ford fractured his leg while filming at Pinewood after a hydraulic door on the <i>Millennium Falcon</i> set fell on him, and was taken to a hospital. According to Abrams, Ford's ankle "went to a 90-degree angle."<sup id="cite_ref-Hiatt_94-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiatt-94">[94]</a></sup> Production was suspended for two weeks to accommodate Ford's injury.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> Ford's son Ben stated that Ford's ankle would likely need a plate and screws and that filming could be altered slightly, with the crew needing to shoot Ford from the waist up for a short time until he recovered.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jake_Steinfeld" title="Jake Steinfeld">Jake Steinfeld</a>, Ford's personal trainer, said in July that Ford was recovering rapidly.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup> Abrams also fractured a vertebra in his own back when he was trying to help lift the door after Ford's accident.<sup id="cite_ref-Hiatt_94-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiatt-94">[94]</a></sup> However, he kept this to himself and did not tell anyone about it for over a month.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> In February 2016 it was reported that the <a href="/wiki/Health_and_Safety_Executive" title="Health and Safety Executive">Health and Safety Executive</a> brought four criminal charges against Disney subsidiary Foodles Production (UK) Ltd for alleged <a href="/wiki/Occupational_safety_and_health" title="Occupational safety and health">health and safety</a> breaches relating to Ford's accident.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>One of the film's storyboard artists, Simon Duric, said "The security on the film was a challenge. That script was locked in a safe. Most of the time on a film you can sit at your desk with a copy of the script next to you. On this, you couldn’t. That’s fine but it was tricky in places. We had people flying drones over Pinewood studios trying to take photographs. It was nuts. If a prop was being moved we had to have them covered in a big black sheet. We were told in an email to be [wary] of drones."<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In July 2014, filming took place over three days at <a href="/wiki/Skellig_Michael" title="Skellig Michael">Skellig Michael</a> island off the coast of <a href="/wiki/County_Kerry" title="County Kerry">County Kerry</a>, Ireland, with a cast including Mark Hamill and Daisy Ridley.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup> Production was halted for two weeks in early August 2014 so Abrams could rework shooting in Ford's absence and resumed with a fully healed Ford during mid-August.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup> In September 2014, the former <a href="/wiki/RAF_Greenham_Common" title="RAF Greenham Common">RAF Greenham Common</a> military base in <a href="/wiki/Berkshire" title="Berkshire">Berkshire</a>, was used as a filming location and featured set constructions of several spaceships from the <i>Star Wars</i> Universe.<sup id="cite_ref-bbc-greenham_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-greenham-166">[166]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Puzzlewood" title="Puzzlewood">Puzzlewood</a> in the Forest of Dean was used as a location for forest scenes.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> Principal photography ended on November 3, 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-production">Post-production</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Post-production">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <div class="thumb tright"> 
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a href="/wiki/File:1221olympicblvd.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1221olympicblvd.jpg/220px-1221olympicblvd.jpg" width="220" height="174" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1221olympicblvd.jpg/330px-1221olympicblvd.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/1221olympicblvd.jpg/440px-1221olympicblvd.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4376" data-file-height="3456"></a> 
       <div class="thumbcaption"> 
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:1221olympicblvd.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
        </div> Bad Robot Productions headquarters in Santa Monica, where Abrams supervised post-production of the film
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p>Cinematographer Daniel Mindel stated that <i>The Force Awakens</i> would use real locations and <a href="/wiki/Miniature_effect" title="Miniature effect">scale models</a> over <a href="/wiki/Computer-generated_imagery" title="Computer-generated imagery">computer-generated imagery</a> to make it aesthetically similar to the original <i>Star Wars</i> trilogy.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Rian_Johnson" title="Rian Johnson">Rian Johnson</a>, director of <i>Episode VIII</i>, reiterated that Abrams would use little CGI and more practical, traditional special effects, saying: "I think people are coming back around to [practical effects]. It feels like there is sort of that gravity pulling us back toward it. I think that more and more people are hitting kind of a critical mass in terms of the CG-driven action scene lending itself to a very specific type of action scene, where physics go out the window and it becomes so big so quick."<sup id="cite_ref-THRJohnson_172-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-THRJohnson-172">[172]</a></sup> Abrams' intention in prioritizing practical special effects was to recreate the visual realism and authenticity of the original <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars_(film)" title="Star Wars (film)">Star Wars</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-effects_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-effects-173">[173]</a></sup> To that end, the droid <a href="/wiki/BB-8" title="BB-8">BB-8</a> was a physical prop that was developed by <a href="/wiki/Disney_Research" title="Disney Research">Disney Research</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Fortune_BB-8_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fortune_BB-8-174">[174]</a></sup> created by special effects artist <a href="/wiki/Neal_Scanlan" title="Neal Scanlan">Neal Scanlan</a> and operated live on set with the actors.<sup id="cite_ref-BB-8_175-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BB-8-175">[175]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Scanlan_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scanlan-176">[176]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>In February 2014, <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic" title="Industrial Light &amp; Magic">Industrial Light &amp; Magic</a> (ILM) announced plans to open a facility in London, citing Disney's <i>Star Wars</i> films as a catalyst for the expansion. ILM's Vancouver branch will also work on the special effects for the film.<sup id="cite_ref-ILM_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ILM-177">[177]</a></sup></p> 
     <p>Abrams supervised post-production and editing of the film at Bad Robot Productions' headquarters in Santa Monica.<sup id="cite_ref-Hiatt_94-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hiatt-94">[94]</a></sup> In August 2015, Abrams gave the estimated running time of the film as 124–125 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">[178]</a></sup> Abrams made changes to the film's plot in the editing process to simplify the film, by removing some sequences shown in trailers: "At one point, Maz used to continue along with the characters back to the Resistance base, but we realised that she really had nothing to do there of value, except to be sitting around."<sup id="cite_ref-Independent_179-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Independent-179">[179]</a></sup> The film was converted to 3D in post-production.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Music">Music</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Music">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
     <div role="note" class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
